\DoxyCodeLine{2028     \textcolor{comment}{// implementation detail: ShortString can represent zero-\/terminated strings up to MaxSize chars}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2029     \textcolor{comment}{// (excluding the terminating zero) and store a value to determine the length of the contained}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2030     \textcolor{comment}{// string in the last character str[LenPos] by storing "{}MaxSize -\/ length"{} there. If the string}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2031     \textcolor{comment}{// to store has the maximal length of MaxSize then str[LenPos] will be 0 and therefore act as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2032     \textcolor{comment}{// the string terminator as well. For getting the string length back from that value just use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2033     \textcolor{comment}{// "{}MaxSize -\/ str[LenPos]"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2034     \textcolor{comment}{// This allows to store 13-\/chars strings in 32-\/bit mode, 21-\/chars strings in 64-\/bit mode,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2035     \textcolor{comment}{// 13-\/chars strings for RAPIDJSON\_48BITPOINTER\_OPTIMIZATION=1 inline (for `UTF8`-\/encoded strings).}}
